{\footnotesize\ttfamily const C\+U\+R\+L\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+N\+E\+C\+T\+\_\+\+O\+N\+LY 141}

5.\+5 \mbox{\hyperlink{patch2_8txt_a3f9992ab8fa942ed02faa63682c3a84c}{{\bfseries{T\+R\+UE}} tells the library to perform all the required proxy authentication and connection setup, but no data transfer. This option is implemented for H\+T\+TP, S\+M\+TP and P\+O\+P3. }}

\mbox{\hyperlink{class_a}{A}} bitmask consisting of one or more of {\bfseries{C\+U\+R\+L\+S\+S\+H\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+U\+B\+L\+I\+C\+K\+EY}}, {\bfseries{C\+U\+R\+L\+S\+S\+H\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+P\+A\+S\+S\+W\+O\+RD}}, {\bfseries{C\+U\+R\+L\+S\+S\+H\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+H\+O\+ST}}, {\bfseries{C\+U\+R\+L\+S\+S\+H\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+K\+E\+Y\+B\+O\+A\+RD}}. Set to {\bfseries{C\+U\+R\+L\+S\+S\+H\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+H\+\_\+\+A\+NY}} to let libcurl pick one. \mbox{\Hypertarget{curl__d_8php_acb4bb725114582bb002d52951e591f03}\label{curl__d_8php_acb4bb725114582bb002d52951e591f03}}
